Examples of categories are 3 of a kind, 4 of a kind, straight, full house, etc. Each player tries to fill in a score for each category, but this is not always possible. When players have entered a score or a zero for all 13 categories, the game ends and total scores are compared.\r\n \r\nSpecial Yahtzee rule is, the first time you get a Yahtzee in a game it is worth 50 points (if you use it in the Yahtzee slot). If you roll another Yahtzee after you have already got the 50 points (i.e., you didn’t take a zero), you will get a 100 point bonus.\r\n\r\nYahtzee is also popularly called Yachty, Yatzie, Yatzee, Yathzy and Poker Dice.\r\n\r\nRoll it to the limit for the ultimate win with the Yahtzee Classic game. \r\n \r\nCan you rack up bonus points by scoring an extra Yahtzee.\r\n \r\nSo, how will you roll?
